PUBLIC NOTICE
I, S. Rajasekar, born as male child to M. Sekar on 2nd May 1985 have been residing at 2/54A, Sanjeevirayan Koil,
Edamanal (Post), Sirkali Taluk, Nagapattinam-609 115. After the Biological change a Sex reassignment Surgery was
performed from Male to Female and has been living as a female. (Reference: Prof. Dr. Soundararajan, M.S., M.Ch, FICS,
FIMSA, Kannan Hospital, No. 17, Bashyam Street, Cuddalore-607 001) The clinical examination under the reference above
also shown that, I could live as a female. Hence I, S. Rajasekar shall henceforth be known as Anusha.

Cuddalore,

S. RAJASEKAR.

9th July 2012.
